[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ## Description                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - Issue without speculation                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           During a fuzzing session, the Jazzer instrumentation raised a critical security   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         alert [1m([0m`FuzzerSecurityIssueCritical: File path traversal`[1m)[0m. The stack trace shows   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         that the violation was detected in the file path traversal sanitizer                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1m([0m`FilePathTraversal.check`[1m)[0m, invoked via the hook                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `FilePathTraversal.pathFirstArgHook` on calls made by                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `[1;35morg.apache.commons.compress.archivers.examples.Expander.expand[0m[1m([0m[33m...[0m[1m)[0m`. The fuzzer   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         harness [1m([0m`ExpanderFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput`[1m)[0m passed malformed archive data which,  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         when processed by the Expander example, attempted to create or overwrite a file     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         using a path that escaped the designated output directory.                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - Vulnerability type                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           Path traversal [1m([0malso known as “directory traversal”[1m)[0m. An attacker-provided        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         archive entry name contained sequences [1m([0me.g., “..[35m/[0m”[1m)[0m that caused output files to be [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         written outside the expected sandbox directory.                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - Important observations and findings                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           • The sanitizer stopped execution at `FilePathTraversal.check` in                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `com.code_intelligence.jazzer.sanitizers`.                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           • The path in question [1m([0m`[35m/tmp/[0m[95mexpander-[0m…[35m/output/q/r/[0m[95mjazzer-traversal[0m`[1m)[0m indicates  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         nested directories introduced by the fuzzer’s synthetic input.                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           • The Expander implementation uses multiple overloaded `expand` methods [1m([0mlines    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m86[0m, [1;36m204[0m, [1;36m324[0m, [1;36m400[0m, [1;36m460[0m[1m)[0m, suggesting a recursive or iterative descent through        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         archive entries.                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           • The harness [1m([0m`ExpanderFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput`[1m)[0m serves only as an entry       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         point; it is not the root cause. The core logic under test resides in the Expander  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         example and its handling of entry names.                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - Code areas to investigate                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           [1;36m1[0m. `[1;35morg.apache.commons.compress.archivers.examples.Expander.expand[0m[1m([0m[33m...[0m[1m)[0m` – All    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         overloads, especially the code that resolves archive entry names to file system     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         paths.                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           [1;36m2[0m. Entry normalization and sanitization logic inside Expander [1m([0me.g., how “..[35m/[0m”    [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [32m'%s'"[0m[39m, parentPath, name, outputFile[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1490[0m[39m:        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1491[0m[39m:        return [0m[1;35mparentPath.resolve[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mNormalizer.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[39mname, [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mNormalizer.Form.NFKD[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1492[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msrc/main/java/org/apache/commons/compress/archivers/examples/Expander.jav[0m[1;92ma:68[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m93[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m68[0m[39m:            throws IOException [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m69[0m[39m:        final boolean nullTarget = targetDirectory == null;[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m70[0m[39m:        final Path targetDirPath = nullTarget ? null : [0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mtargetDirectory.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m71[0m[39m:        T nextEntry = [0m[1;35msupplier.get[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m72[0m[39m:        while [0m[1;39m([0m[39mnextEntry != null[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m73[0m[39m:            final Path targetPath = nullTarget ? null : [0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mnextEntry.resolveIn[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtargetDirPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m74[0m[39m:            if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mnextEntry.isDirectory[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m75[0m[39m:                if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m!nullTarget && ![0m[1;35mFiles.isDirectory[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtargetPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m && [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mFiles.createDirectories[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtargetPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m == null[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m76[0m[39m:                    throw new [0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Failed to create directory "[0m[39m + [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtargetPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m77[0m[39m:                [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m78[0m[39m:            [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m else [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m79[0m[39m:                final Path parent = nullTarget ? null : [0m[1;35mtargetPath.getParent[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m80[0m[39m:                if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m!nullTarget && ![0m[1;35mFiles.isDirectory[0m[1;39m([0m[39mparent[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m && [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mFiles.createDirectories[0m[1;39m([0m[39mparent[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m == null[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m81[0m[39m:                    throw new [0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Failed to create directory "[0m[39m + [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparent[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m82[0m[39m:                [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m83[0m[39m:                if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mnullTarget[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m84[0m[39m:                    [0m[1;35mwriter.accept[0m[1;39m([0m[39mnextEntry, NullOutputStream.INSTANCE[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m85[0m[39m:                [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m else [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m86[0m[39m:                    try [0m[1;39m([0m[39mOutputStream outputStream = [0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mFiles.newOutputStream[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtargetPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m87[0m[39m:                        [0m[1;35mwriter.accept[0m[1;39m([0m[39mnextEntry, outputStream[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m88[0m[39m:                    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m89[0m[39m:                [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m90[0m[39m:            [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m91[0m[39m:            nextEntry = [0m[1;35msupplier.get[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m92[0m[39m:        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m93[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Root-Cause & Impact Analysis  [0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The Expander example’s unsafe [0m[1;35moverload[0m[1;39m([0m[39ms[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m compute output file paths via `new [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mFile[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdestDir, [0m[1;35mentry.getName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mor equivalent unguarded [0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mPath.resolve[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mentry.getName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m without verifying that the normalized path remains[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munder the intended target directory. This permits archive entries with “..[0m[35m/[0m[39m” [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msequences [0m[1;39m([0m[39mor absolute names[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to write outside the sandbox, triggering Jazzer’s [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mFilePathTraversal sanitizer.  [0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The code paths under test are the example methods that open an archive [0m[1;39m([0m[39mZIP or[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mauto-detected format[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, iterate entries, and immediately write them via raw file [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAPIs. Although Commons Compress’s `ArchiveEntry` now provides a safe [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mresolveIn[0m[1;39m([0m[39mPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` helper in recent versions, the Expander example does not [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconsistently use it.  [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Critical Logic to Preserve  [0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - All existing overloads of `[0m[1;35mExpander.expand[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` must still open the archive, [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39miterate entries in the correct order, create directories and copy data.  [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Existing behavior for “null” targets [0m[1;39m([0m[39mwriting to `[0m[35m/dev/[0m[95mnull[0m[39m` or `NUL`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m must be[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mretained.  [0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The Unicode-normalization step for ZIP entries [0m[1;39m([0m[39mpresent in [0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`ZipArchiveEntry.resolveIn`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m should continue to apply.  [0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Fix Strategy Overview  [0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   A. Consolidate all file-writing overloads to the generic [0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m“supplier+writer+resolveIn” core loop, which inherently uses a safe path [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mresolution.  [0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   B. For any remaining overloads or manual loops that still use `new [0m[1;35mFile[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` or[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munchecked `[0m[1;35mresolve[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, replace those blocks with calls into the generic method [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mor inline the same safe resolution logic:  [0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. Convert `File targetDirectory` to `Path targetDirPath = [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mtoPath[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtargetDirectory[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`  [0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. For each `ArchiveEntry entry`, compute  [0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           ```  [0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           Path outputPath = [0m[1;35mentry.resolveIn[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtargetDirPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;  [0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           ```  [0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         catching any `IOException` from `resolveIn` and bubbling it up [0m[1;39m([0m[39mto abort [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mon zip-slip attempts[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. If `[0m[1;35mentry.isDirectory[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, call `[0m[1;35mFiles.createDirectories[0m[1;39m([0m[39moutputPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.  [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         Else, call `[0m[1;35mFiles.createDirectories[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35moutputPath.getParent[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` then open [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mFiles.newOutputStream[0m[1;39m([0m[39moutputPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` and copy data.  [0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   C. Remove or deprecate any legacy example code paths that bypass `resolveIn`, [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mensuring only the hardened path-sanitizing approach remains.  [0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Detailed Patch Steps  [0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. Identify `Expander.java` methods outside the generic `<T extends [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mArchiveEntry>` overload [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., `[0m[1;35mexpand[0m[1;39m([0m[39mPath archive, Path targetDirectory[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mexpand[0m[1;39m([0m[39mFile archive, File targetDirectory[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, and any ZIP-specific loops[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. In each, replace the manual loop that reads `ArchiveEntry entry = [0m[33m...[0m[39m; while [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mentry != null[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m[39m [0m[33m...[0m[39m [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m` and the construction  [0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         `File f = new [0m[1;35mFile[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdestDir, [0m[1;35mentry.getName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`  [0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      with a delegate call to the generic core:  [0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         ```java[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m old:[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         ArchiveInputStream in = new [0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mZipArchiveInputStream[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mFiles.newInputStream[0m[1;39m([0m[39marchivePath[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m manual loop writing to File f[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m [0m[33m...[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m new:[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[1;35mexpand[0m[1;39m([0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m -> [0m[1;39m{[0m[39m [0m[35m/[0m[39m* supplier: getNextEntry with canReadEntryData check *[0m[35m/[0m[39m [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m,[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           [0m[1;39m([0m[39mentry, out[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m -> [0m[1;35mIOUtils.copy[0m[1;39m([0m[39min, out[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m,[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           targetDirPath[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         ```  [0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      or inline the safe resolution block if delegation is undesirable.  [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. Ensure that `[0m[1;35mtoPath[0m[1;39m([0m[39mFile[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` remains a thin wrapper around `[0m[1;35mfile.toPath[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` and [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mis used everywhere.  [0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. Remove any direct calls to `[0m[1;35mgetParentFile[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.mkdirs[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` or `new [0m[1;35mFile[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` in [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe example code. Replace them with `[0m[1;35mFiles.createDirectories[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` on the [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnormalized `Path`.  [0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m. Add JavaDoc or comments pointing at `ArchiveEntry.resolveIn` for future [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmaintainers.  [0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Justification & Safety  [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - By routing all entry-writing logic through the interface’s `resolveIn` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mwhich [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnormalizes, checks prefix, and applies Unicode normalization for ZIP formats[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, we [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39meliminate directory-traversal vulnerabilities once and for all.  [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The generic loop already preserves all existing functionality: directory [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcreation, NUL/`NullOutputStream` behavior for `nullTarget`, and correct stream [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcopying.  [0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We are not modifying any harness/fuzzing code or external libraries—only the [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mExpander example. Existing unit and manual tests against Expander will continue to [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpass, since behavior for well-formed archives is unchanged.  [0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Potential Side Effects & Mitigation  [0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - On archives that relied on writing outside the target directory [0m[1;39m([0m[39man unintended[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbehavior[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, expand will now abort with `[0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Zip slip …"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`. This is a [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msecurity‐hardening change, deemed acceptable for an example tool.  [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - If downstream code catches `IOException` and swallows it, the example may [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mterminate earlier; documentation should be updated to highlight that ZIP-slip [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mattempts are treated as errors.  [0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Regression: Ensure that archives with deeply nested directories [0m[1;39m([0m[39mbut still [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munder the target[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m remain writable. The `[0m[1;35mnormalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.startsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` check permits [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnested under the base directory.  [0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7[0m[39m. Verification  [0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Add a small positive test: archive with `dir/..[0m[35m/../target/[0m[95mfoo[0m[39m` should now [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthrow `IOException` rather than writing.  [0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Run Jazzer fuzz harness again; the `FuzzerSecurityIssueCritical` for [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpath-traversal should no longer fire.  [0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Confirm examples still expand valid archives as before.  [0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAn example archiver “Expander” triggered a Jazzer security finding [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`FuzzerSecurityIssueCritical`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m for file-path traversal when extracting archives. A[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mproposed patch replaced the archive-detection call [0m[1;39m([0m[39musing [0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`ArchiveStreamFactory.detect`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m with a try-with-resources block creating an [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`ArchiveInputStream` directly and removed several NIO channel imports. After [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mapplying this patch, the Java compiler reported multiple errors: missing symbols [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`SeekableByteChannel`, `FileChannel`, `Channels`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, name clashes between overloaded[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`expand` methods, and ambiguous method references.[0m                                  [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Initial Issue[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- A fuzzer input caused the `[0m[1;35mExpander.expand[0m[1;39m([0m[39mPath, Path[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method to invoke [0m         [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The exception stack traces back to calls in:[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • `[0m[1;35mExpander.expand[0m[1;39m([0m[39m…, Path[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`  [0m                                                    [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdoes not sanitize extracted file paths before writing to disk.[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Patch Attempt[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- In `Expander.java`, the single-argument `[0m[1;35mexpand[0m[1;39m([0m[39mPath archive, Path [0m               [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`ArchiveStreamFactory`.  [0m                                                           [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      `[0m[1;35mexpand[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mArchiveStreamFactory.detect[0m[1;39m([0m[39minputStream[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, archive, targetDirectory[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    with:[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         allows path traversal [1m([0mentries escaping the target directory[1m)[0m.                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m. Observations from the Initial Issue                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - The stack trace shows the vulnerability check failing in the sanitization hook [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         for file paths.                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - The vulnerable code path originates in `Expander.expand` methods which accept  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         various archive formats [1m([0mZIP, TAR, 7z[1m)[0m via both `InputStream` and                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `SeekableByteChannel` overloads.                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - The harness [1m([0m`ExpanderFuzzer`[1m)[0m calls `[1;35mexpand[0m[1m([0mformat, archivePath, targetDir[1m)[0m`. [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m. Patch Attempt                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - Imports for NIO channels [1m([0m`FileChannel`, `SeekableByteChannel`, `Channels`,    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `StandardOpenOption`[1m)[0m were removed.                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - Two-argument `[1;35mexpand[0m[1m([0mPath archive, Path targetDirectory[1m)[0m` was rewritten to     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         chain through `ArchiveStreamFactory.createArchiveInputStream`.                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - All `[1;35mexpand[0m[1m([0mString format, SeekableByteChannel archive, …[1m)[0m` overloads          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1m([0mincluding those using `TarFile`, `ZipFile`, `SevenZFile`[1m)[0m were deleted or          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         commented out.                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - The deprecated two-argument overload taking `SeekableByteChannel` was removed  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         entirely.                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - The goal was to unify on a single streaming API and eliminate code paths that  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         bypassed path-traversal sanitization.                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m. Patch Result and Logs                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - Maven compilation failed with two errors in `Expander.java`:                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              * Cannot find symbol `SeekableByteChannel` at a still-present reference on     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         line [1;36m362[0m.                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              * Ambiguous call to `[1;35mexpand[0m[1m([0mString, InputStream, File, CloseableConsumer[1m)[0m` vs. [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `[1;35mexpand[0m[1m([0mString, SeekableByteChannel, File, CloseableConsumer[1m)[0m` on line [1;36m262[0m.         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - These errors indicate residual references or overloads to                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `SeekableByteChannel` were not fully removed, and signature collisions arose after  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         deleting methods.                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m. Areas for Further Investigation                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - `Expander.java` method signatures and imports: ensure all references to        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `SeekableByteChannel` and related overloads are consistently removed or updated.    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - Calls to `[1;35mexpand[0m[1m([0m[33m...[0m[1m)[0m` in the same file [1m([0maround lines [1;36m262[0m and [1;36m362[0m[1m)[0m that now    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         refer to nonexistent or ambiguous methods.                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - Use of `CloseableConsumer` and deprecated methods to verify that proper        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         overloads remain and that no ambiguous signatures exist.                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - Build and API dependencies: confirm whether downstream or upstream code        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         expects `SeekableByteChannel`-based expansion entry points.                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m             at [1;35mExpander.expand[0m[1m([0mExpander.jav[1;92ma:86[0m[1m)[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m             [33m...[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m             at [1;35mExpanderFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput[0m[1m([0mExpanderFuzzer.jav[1;92ma:52[0m[1m)[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           ```                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - This indicates that during archive expansion, a crafted input allowed extraction  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         of entries with path components that traverse upwards [1m([0me.g., `..[35m/[0m`[1m)[0m, writing files  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         outside the intended target directory.                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         Patch Attempt                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - In `Expander.java`, the two public `[1;35mexpand[0m[1m([0mPath, Path[1m)[0m` and `[1;35mexpand[0m[1m([0mString, Path, [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         Path[1m)[0m` methods were modified to open the archive as an `ArchiveInputStream`         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         directly:                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           ```diff                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            public void [1;35mexpand[0m[1m([0mfinal Path archive, final Path targetDirectory[1m)[0m throws        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         IOException, ArchiveException [1m{[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         -      try [1m([0mInputStream in = [1;35mFiles.newInputStream[0m[1m([0marchive[1m)[0m[1m)[0m [1m{[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         -          [1;35mexpand[0m[1m([0m[1;35mdetect[0m[1m([0min[1m)[0m, archive, targetDirectory[1m)[0m;                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         +      try [1m([0mInputStream in = [1;35mFiles.newInputStream[0m[1m([0marchive[1m)[0m;                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         +           ArchiveInputStream ain = [1;35mFactory.DEFAULT.createArchiveInputStream[0m[1m([0min[1m)[0m[1m)[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1m{[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         +          [1;35mexpand[0m[1m([0main, targetDirectory[1m)[0m;                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                [1m}[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            [1m}[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           ```                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - All overloads accepting `SeekableByteChannel` [1m([0mwith and without                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `CloseableConsumer`[1m)[0m and those deprecated or leaking resources were removed and     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         replaced with comments like                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           ```java                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           [35m/[0m[35m/[0m Deprecated seekable-channel overload removed                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           ```                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - Imports and methods related to `Channels`, `FileChannel`, `SeekableByteChannel`,  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         and `StandardOpenOption` were deleted.                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         Patch Result                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - Running the Maven build with `japicmp` produced incompatibility errors due to     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         removed methods and changed exception signatures:                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           ```                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           METHOD_REMOVED:                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m             [1;35mExpander.expand[0m[1m([0mString, SeekableByteChannel, File[1m)[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m             [1;35mExpander.expand[0m[1m([0mString, SeekableByteChannel, File, CloseableConsumer[1m)[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m             [1;35mExpander.expand[0m[1m([0mString, SeekableByteChannel, Path, CloseableConsumer[1m)[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           METHOD_NO_LONGER_THROWS_CHECKED_EXCEPTION [35m/[0m METHOD_NOW_THROWS_CHECKED_EXCEPTION:  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m             [1;35mCLI.main[0m[1m([0mString[1m[[0m[1m][0m[1m)[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m             [1;35mByteCode.extractOperands[0m[1m([0m[33m...[0m[1m)[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m             [1;35mCodeAttribute.CodeAttribute[0m[1m([0m[33m...[0m[1m)[0m                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m             [1;35mNewClassRefForm.setByteCodeOperands[0m[1m([0m[33m...[0m[1m)[0m                                        [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m           ```                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - These API breaks caused the build to fail, as the binary interface no longer      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         matched the previous release.                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         Areas for Further Investigation                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - The behavior of all `[1;35mexpand[0m[1m([0mArchiveInputStream, Path[1m)[0m` code paths, especially     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         entry‐extraction loops and path normalization logic, to understand where traversal  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         checks are applied or missing.                                                      [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         other examples [1m([0me.g., TAR, ZIP, 7z handlers[1m)[0m.                                       [2m                [0m
